		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '03bedb6eb0d63556f89f5cb5160c5ff0c2a186c6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '03bedb6eb0d63556f89f5cb5160c5ff0c2a186c6') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3dcb01c82daada503bfe85159554291e63573cde') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '03bedb6eb0d63556f89f5cb5160c5ff0c2a186c6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_35();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml') !== 'fda568dce41c86ccec76ffb45b8ad3b890479411') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_36();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'cbb6ffc65c394c360460c6b2d7a2bf2005a8aea7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'cbb6ffc65c394c360460c6b2d7a2bf2005a8aea7') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '605337f88fe510f8215c9ed6d0416e0f29918aa6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_36();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'cbb6ffc65c394c360460c6b2d7a2bf2005a8aea7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml') != '2a353c5f6ea43f7a4d4b177b00608662f000270b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml') !== '2a353c5f6ea43f7a4d4b177b00608662f000270b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml') !== 'd0aeafd50b5602cc1db657c082a23169fbd78f6b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_78();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml') !== '2a353c5f6ea43f7a4d4b177b00608662f000270b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/sqlSlang/pgsql/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}
